  102|       | * Creates a new TreeTable based on the specified TreeTableConf struct and returns
  103|       | * a status code.
  104|       | *
  105|       | * The table is allocated using the memory allocators specified in the TreeTableConf
  106|       | * struct.
  107|       | *

  109|       | * @param[out] out Pointer to where the newly created TreeTable is stored

  114|       |enum cc_stat treetable_new_conf(TreeTableConf const * const conf, TreeTable **tt)

  117|       |

  119|      0|        return CC_ERR_ALLOC;
  120|       |
  121|     47|    RBNode *sentinel = conf->mem_calloc(1, sizeof(RBNode));
  122|       |
  123|     47|    if (!sentinel) {
  124|      0|        conf->mem_free(table);
  125|      0|        return CC_ERR_ALLOC;

  135|     47|    table->root       = sentinel;
